+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""
+Tests for Ralph's Math Helper
+"""
+
+import subprocess
+import sys
+
+
+def run_ralph_math(arg1, arg2):
+    """Helper function to run ralph_math.py with given arguments."""
+    result = subprocess.run(
+        [sys.executable, "ralph_math.py", str(arg1), str(arg2)],
+        capture_output=True,
+        text=True
+    )
+    return result.stdout.strip(), result.returncode
+
+
+def test_simple_addition():
+    """Test case: 2 + 2 = 4 (should succeed)"""
+    output, returncode = run_ralph_math(2, 2)
+    assert "4 ... I calculate good!" in output, f"Expected '4 ... I calculate good!' but got '{output}'"
+    assert returncode == 0, f"Expected return code 0 but got {returncode}"
+    print("✓ Test passed: 2 + 2 = 4")
+
+
+def test_sum_equals_10():
+    """Test case: 5 + 5 = 10 (boundary case, should succeed)"""
+    output, returncode = run_ralph_math(5, 5)
+    assert "10 ... I calculate good!" in output, f"Expected '10 ... I calculate good!' but got '{output}'"
+    assert returncode == 0, f"Expected return code 0 but got {returncode}"
+    print("✓ Test passed: 5 + 5 = 10")
+
+
+def test_sum_greater_than_10():
+    """Test case: 5 + 6 = 11 (should be unpossible)"""
+    output, returncode = run_ralph_math(5, 6)
+    assert "That is unpossible!" in output, f"Expected 'That is unpossible!' but got '{output}'"
+    print("✓ Test passed: 5 + 6 is unpossible")
+
+
+def test_large_sum():
+    """Test case: 100 + 200 = 300 (should be unpossible)"""
